<P>{@sAraLA mahAbhArata

<P>y1ethu anantare baibasuta manu rAjA

<P>agasti muniMka caraNe kalAka dibya pUjA | 1 |

<P>azwamedha yAga kruSNa swargArohaNa uttAreNa kathA

<P>kahibA bho ruSi mote pANDabaMka byabasthA | 2 |

<P1>prathama dhADire nimnalikhita bhinma bhinma pothire bhinma pATha :--

<P1>y1ethu anantare bilaMka deza rAjA

<P1>agastiMka padmapAde kale dibya pUjA |

<P1>nistarili muni tumbhara bAkya zuNi

<P1>y1ethu anantare kathAy1e kaha brahmamuni |

<P1>bauda rUpe kruSNa nILagirire bijekaLe

<P1>tahuMNa pANDaba ye kebaNa krutya kale |+

<P1>badanti agasti zuNimA brahmamuni

<P1>yujheSThi debe rAjya pUjA gheni |

<P1>aneka Ay1ojana ye ratnamAna dile

<P1>samasta rAjya prajAMku binoy1I kahile |

<P1>agasti bolanti zuNa bilaMka nrupamaNi

<P1>y1ethu anantare zuNa swargArohaNa bANI | �Ta, jha, cha� pothi

[MBO-11(3)-2]

<P>agasti boile ho sAbadhAne zuNa

<P>mahAbhAratha ante ye swarga ArohaNa | 3 |

<P>kathay1anti mahAtamA agasti yurANa brahmaruSi

<P>kaLiyuga prabeza ye hoilAka Asi | 4 |

<P>anIti gati loke hele garuhaMsI

<P>kaLiyuga siddha ye abhay1e somabaMzI | 5 |

<P>driyodhana mAri rAjya kale kaLiyugara madhye

<P>AThazata baraSa helA y1eNe kruSNa gale badhe | 6 |

<P>kruSNara galA uttAre baraSa zata dui

<P>rAjya karuchanti ye pANDaba pAn~chabhai | 7 |

<P>y1e kSetra mahIbhAra rAjyara sampada

<P>kesaneka yujheSthi kale bana sadha | 8 |

<P>kaha mahAmuni mote swarga ArohaNa bANI

<P>agasti boile ho zuNa nrupamaNi | 9 |

<P>rAtra prabhAteNa AstAne bijay1e daNDadhArI

<P>yujheSThi debe sakaLa jananta hakAri | 10 |

<P>pAtra mantrI amanAtya sanya ye prohita

<P>rAiNa bacana ye bolanti dharmasuta | 11 |

<P>bAbu tumbhe sakaLa jane zuNimA mora bANI

<P>AmbhaMku sakhA thile deba catrapANi | 12 |

<P>kruSNara abhAbe Ambhaera kisa rAjya

<P>kahai tumbhanta yebe Ambhara pUrba kAryya | 13 |

<P>yeteka doSa tumbhanta achai kari

<P>kSamA karibAka y1ebe se doSa mohori | 14 |

<P>mohora apamAna pAila bahuta

<P>y1e doSa mohora kSamA karibA samasta | 15 |

<P1>8|2 yesaneke yujheSThi bacana paramAda |(ka)

[MBO-11(3)-3]

<P>samasta doSa mora karibA upekSA

<P>kin~chita puNye mor abahuta dharma bAn~cchA | 16 |

<P>mahatwa prANImAne na ghenanti doSa

<P>kin~chita loke ye bujhanti bizeSa | 17 |

<P>mote AjahuM tumbhe upekSA karibA

<P>paboGgkSa anumate sakaLe rahibA | 18 |

<P>candreNa yesane aTai tArA ye bidita

<P>tesaneka hoi nare tumbhara niy1ata | 19 |

<P>y1e mohora lakSmI yebe parIkSaku dei

<P>baneNa gamana karibuM pan~chu bhAi | 20 |

<P>yujheSThi bacana zuNi samasta bismay1a mana

<P>Ambhanta chaDi nrupati kAhiMki karibu gabana | 21 |

<P>Ambhe bane yAi samaste tumbhanta karibuM sebA

<P>anurAga keteka achai AgyAM debA | 22 |

<P>baday1anti yujheSThi nirmaLa y1ehu bANI

<P>rAjya kara tumbhe parIkSaku gheni | 23 |

<P>mote yete bhagati parIkSaku debA

<P>tAhAra yete doSa kale mote upekSibA | 24 |

<P>parIkSaku rAjya dile hastinA nagarI

<P>pan~chu kaTaka madhye y1ekAGga daNDadhArI | 25 |

<P>pAtra bruhasena mantrI somadAsa

<P>rAjyara subidhAna karanti sarba yaza | 26 |

<P>parIkSaku tiAranti deba dharma ziSe

<P>bAbu prajA pALile barddhuta hoai yazazrI Ay1uSe | 27 |

<P1>27|2 parajAMku yeuM rAjA pALaiTi dharme
<>ariSThi abidhi na thAi deba dharme |[abaziSTAMza para pruSThAre]

[MBO-11(3)-4]

<P>parajAku yebaNa rAjA pALai putra tule

<P>deba indra tahim pALaiTi bhale | 28 |

<P>rAjA pALile se parajA hoi susta

<P>prajA pALane kruSi upujai bahuta | 29 |

<P>kruSi upujile bhaNDAra hoy1e puSTa

<P>jaLa jantumAne na pAbanti kaSTa | 30 |

<P>ApaNe zrIkare mApile yujheSThi

<P>aSTAdaza hAtha hoilA naLakAThi | 31 |

<P>dIrgha pan~chabiMza prati pan~chabiMza naLa uThi

<P>y1emanta ghana karante hoiba y1eka bATi | 32 |

<P>y1ethaku kara bhiANa kale seTi

<P>bATikare saMjA ghenima y1eka ye pauTi | 33 |

<P>yujheSThi debe kahile rAjyara bidhAna

<P>yatane kahile samasta rAjyara subidhAna kathAmAna | 34 |

<P>sujana dekhile niyoga deuthibu

<P>jIba thibAyAy1e tAhAku na huDibu | 35 |

<P>tAhAra antare debu puaku adhikAra

<P>yujheSThi deba tiArile aneka bebhAra | 36 |

<P>saMcapi kahile ye aneka bidhAna

<P>antakari pAribA ki paThana lekhana | 37 |

<P>y1emantara samay1e baitaraNI nadI kULe

<P>bedapura boli ye nagra parimaLe | 38 |

<P1>parajAMku yebaNa rAjA pALai samatule

<P1>deba indra se rAjye pALai jANa bhale |(cha)

<P1>28|2 kSetara taTaku kara y1eka tule |(ka, Ta, jha, cha, Da)

[MBO-11(3)-5]

<P>se nagre surezwara boliNa brAhmaNa

<P>y1ekadine prabeza hoile kurSi karmeNa | 39 |

<P>taDapA boliNa tAhAra kiriSANa

<P>laGgaLa gheniNa se bhUmi karai karaSaNa | 40 |

<P>laGgaLa pheDilA uttAre paNDAy1e dileka kodALa

<P>khetara Tikara khAla kar asamatula | 41 |

<P>y1e budA hANiNa tu pAkAa bhUmiki

<P>kheta sampUrNNa hou bhUmi hou niki | 42 |

<P>AgyAM dei bidujana galA nija pure

<P>khLAi kiriSANa budAi pakAi dUre dUre | 43 |

<P>hANante pASANe yAi bAjilAka koDi

<P>pathara kADhante pAilAka ratna jAli | 44 |

<P>dhana dekhiNa se mahAbaLabantA

<P>mathAre ghenilA se duguNa zakatA | 45 |

<P>muNDiai paNDAMka chamure beta dei

<P>paNDAy1e boile nia yA tohora gharakaiM | 46 |

<P>kruSi se Ambhara nA aTai yugate

<P>karme se yebe pAilu bebhAra aTai tote | 47 |

<P>bolai taDApA gosAiM kahila anIti

<P>tumbhara toTA bAstu tumbhara bADibrutti | 48 |

<P>tumbhara upara baMze kebaNa sAdheba

<P>gupate thoilA Ana ke hariba | 49 |

<P>muhiM kruSikArI upujAibi bitta

<P>dhana mohora kisa mUlyahiM yugata | 50 |

<P>anna basra barttana huai yete mote

<P>tumbhra Ay1e bitta muM nemaiM kemante | 51 |

<P1>40|2 kiriSANa = kruSANa |

<P1>42|2 niki = bhala |

<P1>44|2 pathara kAdhante pAilA ratna jhAli (pAilA ratnatuDi)(Na)

<P1>51|2 tumbhara Ay1e bitta = tumbhara se bitta |

[MBO-11(3)-6]

<P>brAhmaNa bolai tuho zuNasi sampAda

<P>kruSANa hoi mote karai apabAda | 52 |

<P>y1ehAra karme se upujilA bitta

<P>muhiM y1ehA kesaneke karibi grAhita | 53 |

<P>kiriSANa boilA tumbhe puNyabanta jana

<P>y1eteka chanda bandha se tumbhara baDapaNa | 54 |

<P>bAra cinA barttane anna basre muM kAreNi

<P>rAjAra chamure yAiM guhAri karibi y1ehikSaNi | 55 |

<P>brAhmaNa boilA bege mathAre ghena y1ehA

<P>rAjAra chamuku yibA chAlare dorehA | 56 |

<P>Aho caitana brAhmaNa kariSANa duhiMkara kaLi

<P>dhana gheni duheM yujheSThi debaMka chamure yAiM miLi | 57 |

<P>siMghadwAre nei thoileka nidhi

<P>kiriSANa boilA mote hoilA abidhi | 58 |

<P>brAhmaNa boilA deba y1e mohora kiriSANa

<P>y1e mohora upare dekhAucchi chanduALa paNa | 59 |

<P>goLa zabada zuNi bijekale yujheSThi

<P>dekhile siMghadwAre kaNay1a jAli goTi | 60 |

<P>surezwara boilA deba y1e mohora kiriSANa

<P>kodALa dei boili y1e budAmAna hANa | 61 |

<P>hANante tahiMru pAilA y1e amUlya ratna nidhi

<P>bho deba ratna y1ehAra hoibanA bidhi | 62 |

<P>y1eDe chanduALa niki caSAloka hoi

<P>y1ehAra arajilA dhana y1e mohora upare pakAi | 63 |

<P1>56|2 rAjAra chamuku chAla yibA se bichAra karibe yAhA |(ka)

[MBO-11(3)-7]

<P>yujheSThi debe boile yebe pAilu ratnajAli (jhari)

<P>dhana na nei kimpe brAhmaNa tule dwanda kari | 64 |

<P>kiriSANa boilA deba muM karai bepAra

<P>anna basra baratana hoai sinA mora | 65 |

<P>bhUmire yebaNahiM upujai Ay1e

<P>y1ehAMkar ahoi sinA bichAra debarAy1e | 66 |

<P>yujheSThi boile ho adhe adhe kara

<P>bANTinia dhana tumbhe bichAra Ambhara 67 |

<P>kiriSANa boilA deba tumbhe se dharmarAy1e

<P>mohora beLete nei nohai cinAy1e | 68 |

<P>brAhmaNa boilA muM cinAy1e kimpe nebi

<P>y1ehu dukhe arjilA muhiM kesane haribi | 69 |

<P>zuNiNa Azrija hoile yujheSThi nrupabara

<P>sahadebaku boile y1e kebaNa bichAra | 70 |

<P>sahadeba boilA deba bujhibA y1ehikSaNi

<P>y1ethira tadanta muM achainA jANi | 71 |

<P>kaLiyuga prabeza hoilA zuNimA tathya kathA | 72 |

<P>udiyoge zrIkruSNa hoigale dUta

<P>sehidinuM kaLiyuga hoilA udita | 73 |

<P>hari arjunara bhay1eNa pazita nuArilA

<P>mahAbhAratha yuddhe kaLi prabeza hoilA | 74 |

<P>Ambhara samay1e sukha bhoga nimante

<P>kaLiki pazi na dile sahadeba jagannAthe | 75 |

[MBO-11(3)-8]

<P>AkAzara bANI paDilA zuNa he sahadeba

<P>anIti paDibaTi tumbhe na thAa y1eba | 76 |

<P>kruSNa aile arjuna nAhiM swarge

<P>puNa jAta hoibanA kaLiyuga bhoge | 77 |

<P>yujheSThi deba AkAze ye naile nohai

<P>dharmarAjA na thile AkAza na zohai | 78 |

<>rAjAGkara mukti@}

<P>baibasuta muni agastiMki kale pUjA
